    61→
    62→### mudprod Repeat Command
    63→- `/home/mudprod/mud repeat "COMMAND"` - Sets a command to repeat on balance recovery
    64→- `/home/mudprod/mud repeat ""` - Disables the repeat trigger
    65→- Examples:
    66→  - `mud repeat "WEAVE CHARGE PIXIE"` - Auto-attack pixies
    67→  - `mud repeat "WEAVE CHARGE RAT"` - Auto-attack rats
    68→  - `mud repeat "WEAVE CHARGE WARRIOR"` - Target pixie warriors specifically
    69→- **WARNING:** Disable before entering Queen/Lord rooms!
    70→
    71→### Useful Commands
    72→- `WALKTO <landmark>` - Auto-walk to named locations
    73→- `LANDMARKS` - List available landmarks
    74→- `CONFIG COMMANDSEPARATOR |` - Use | to chain commands
    75→- **MAX 2 movement directions at a time** - Avoid "now now" errors
    76→- `GLANCE <direction>` - See what's in adjacent room
    77→- `SHOW LEVEL` - Quick level check
    78→- `DEF` - View current defences
    79→- `AB <skill>` - View abilities in a skill
    80→- `PORTALS` - Emergency escape (limited uses after level 11!)

5.21 Voice or Accent

       5.20 < INFAMY                                      Poses > 5.22


You may either choose a voice, or an accent, in order to express yourself more
fully in Achaea. Choosing a voice clears your accent. Choosing an accent clears
your voice.

In either case, your accent or your voice are part of what you say or, more
specifically, how you say things, and are subject to all of the restrictions in
HELP LANGUAGE RULES.

   SET VOICE  <description>   - chooses your voice. Punctuation marks OK.
   SET ACCENT <description>   - chooses your accent. Punctuation marks OK.

   SET VOICE CLEAR            - clears out both voice and accent altogether.
   SET ACCENT CLEAR           - (same!).

Be very careful on this one. It must be literally 'CLEAR', not 'clear',
[Type MORE if you wish to continue reading. (45% shown)]

4.20 CHARACTER STATISTICS

            | THE FELLOWSHIP OF                                 |
       4.19 < EXPLORERS                                   NAMES > 4.21

(See also HELP STATUS)

Adventurers in Achaea have four stats (or statistics):

Str - Strength     - relates to the physical damage you can deal out.
Dex - Dexterity    - relates to your ability to avoid getting hit in
                     combat along with speed of performing some actions.
Con - Constitution - relates to your maximum health and endurance.
Int - Intelligence - affects your maximum mana and magical damage.

(Each of these stats may affect other things besides what is listed.)

14.6 Achaea History Quest

       14.5 < Honours Quests               The Quest Log System > 14.7

It is said that those who do not learn from the past are doomed to repeat it. The history of Achaea is an epic story spanning generations, and it is best told by those who lived it. Across the lands are seven special entities who have experienced the events that shaped our world. They regale those who visit them with their stories.

To begin your voyage into Achaea's past, seek out Enfrin, the woodcutter in New Thera. This is a multi-step task which will require that you visit several places in Achaea, testing your grasp of basic geography as well as enriching your knowledge of history.
